RCM_amass_local_popular_support_cat = {
	RCM_popular_amass_support_mission = {
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 50 # Stays for 5 days before being removed
		#days_re_enable = 25 # Will show up in the interface and can be selected again after 5 days
		is_good = yes
		allowed = {
			is_literally_china = yes
		}
		
		activation = {
			always = no #activate through scripted gui
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
					country_event = RCM_popular_uprising.5
				}
				JAP = {
					country_event = RCM_popular_uprising.5
				}
			}
			#random_state = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_state_flag = warlord_amass_support_flag_temp
			#	}
			event_target:warlord_amass_support_flag_temp = {
				owner = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									tag = JAP
									tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
								}
							}
						}
						country_event = RCM_popular_uprising.5
					}
				}
				THIS = {
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
				clr_state_flag = warlord_amass_support_flag_temp
				set_state_flag = commie_amassed_support
			}
			add_war_support = 0.005
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:amass_support_flag_temp = {
						WTT_is_potential_political_struggle_state = yes
					}
					has_country_flag = wtt_political_struggle
				}
				#Add random state support for ROOT
				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes

				hidden_effect = {
					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support
					save_event_target_as = state
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }
						}
						save_event_target_as = majority_country
					}

					#Update state support
					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes

					#Status events
					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes

					#Recalc all support
					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:warlord_amass_support_flag_temp = {
				clear_global_event_target = warlord_amass_support_flag_temp
			}
		}
		available = { #can doc
			event_target:warlord_amass_support_flag_temp = {
				NOT = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
	RCM_amass_local_popular_support = {
		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns
		visible = {
			is_chinese_warlord = yes
			any_owned_state = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } #MODDED
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			any_owned_state = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } #MODDED
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = RCM_popular_amass_support_mission
			}
		}
		cost = 50
		#days_remove = 7
		#days_re_enable = 7
		#fire_only_once = yes
		modifier = {

		}
		remove_effect = {

		}
		complete_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } #MODDED
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = warlord_amass_support_flag_temp
			}
			activate_mission = RCM_popular_amass_support_mission
		}
	}
}

	RCM_JAP_game_in_progress_champion_mission = {
		icon = ball
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 60 # Stays for 5 days before being removed
		#days_re_enable = 25 # Will show up in the interface and can be selected again after 5 days
		#cost = 40

		}

		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
		timeout_effect = { #run effect on selection
			custom_effect_tooltip = the_game_result_will_be_announced_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.9	
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = disable_baseball_news_events_flag }
					}
					news_event = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2
				}		
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = autorun_on #I didn't use the opt out flag so the event would run one last time if we turn it off mid game
						}
					}
					country_event = rcmjapan_baseball.9
				}
			}
			activate_mission = RCM_JAP_seasonal_intermission_mission
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = JAP_church_sponsored_baseball_games_focus
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = ballgame_revenue_idea
					days = 60
				}
			}
		}

		}

								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_keio }

								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_hosei }
								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_waseda }
								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_meiji }
								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_tokyo }
							}
						}

							limit = {
								NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_expand_the_Tokyo_Big6_Baseball_League_focus }
							}

								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_keio }

								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_hosei }
								10 = { set_country_flag = champion_is_waseda }
							}
						}					
					}
					news_event = rcmjapan_baseball_news.2
				}
			}	
			activate_mission = RCM_JAP_seasonal_intermission_mission
			if = {
				limit = {

			if = {

RCM_JAP_promote_religious_freedom = {
	RCM_publically_endorse_church_authorities = {
		icon = eng_install_government
		#fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 150
		allowed = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		#target_trigger = {
		#	FROM = {
		#		tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		#	}
		#}
		visible = { #can see
			OR = {
				has_idea = jap_church_1
				has_idea = jap_church_2
				has_idea = jap_church_3
				has_idea = jap_church_4
				has_idea = jap_church_5
			}
			NOT = {
				has_idea = jap_church_6
			}
			has_completed_focus = JAP_fund_the_unitarian_church_focus
		}
		available = { #can do
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = jap_church_1
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_10
					check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance > 10 }
				}				
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = jap_church_2
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_30
					check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance > 30 }
				}				
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = jap_church_3
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_50
					check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance > 50 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = jap_church_4
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_70
					check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance > 70 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = jap_church_5
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = church_acceptance_greater_than_90
					check_variable = { ROOT.current_christian_acceptance > 90 }
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
			country_event = rcmjapan_christian.1
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = jap_church_1
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = jap_church_1
						add_idea = jap_church_2
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = jap_church_2
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = jap_church_2
						add_idea = jap_church_3
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = jap_church_3
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = jap_church_3
						add_idea = jap_church_4
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = jap_church_4
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = jap_church_4
						add_idea = jap_church_5
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = jap_church_5
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = jap_church_5
						add_idea = jap_church_6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort
		}
		modifier = {
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

				tooltip = christian_acceptance_over_35

				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
			set_country_flag = persecution_banned
			custom_effect_tooltip = execute_this_to_increase_acceptance_cap
			
			if = {
				limit = { #low
					NOT = { has_idea = suzuki_bunji }
					NOT = { has_idea = katayama_testu }
				}
				JAP_ban_persecution_15_35_50 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = { #mid
						has_idea = suzuki_bunji
						has_idea = katayama_testu
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = { #high
							has_idea = suzuki_bunji
							has_idea = katayama_testu
						}
					}
				}
				JAP_ban_persecution_20_40_40 = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = { #high
						has_idea = suzuki_bunji
						has_idea = katayama_testu
					}
				}
				JAP_ban_persecution_25_45_30 = yes
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = have_socialist_christian_in_cabinet_can_increase_chance_for_support
		}

		}

		icon = eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 150
		allowed = {
			tag = MAN
		}
		visible = { #can see
			tag = MAN			
			has_completed_focus = MAN_realize_the_white_movement_focus
		}
		available = { #can do
			has_war_with = SOV
			SOV = {
				fascism > 0.4
				exists = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
					has_civil_war = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = JAP
				}
				563 = { is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes }
				561 = { is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes }
				657 = { is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes }
				409 = { is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes }
				408 = { is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes }
				else = {
					controls_state = 563
					controls_state = 561
					controls_state = 657
					controls_state = 409
					controls_state = 408
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_capital = no
						}
					}
				}				
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = RCM_Manchoukuo.18 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_completed_focus = SOV_the_bloc_of_rights_and_trotskyites
						}						
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = fascism
							###only_own_territory = yes
							size = 0.15
							capital = 408
							states = { 408 409 657 561 560 563 }
						}
						puppet_white_russia_MAN = yes
						white_movement_construction_post_purge = yes
						else = {				
							start_civil_war = {
								ideology = fascism
								capital = 408
								states = { 408 409 657 561 560 563 655 564 565 566 }
								size = 0.3
								keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
							}
							puppet_white_russia_MAN = yes
							white_movement_construction_no_purge = yes
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						RFP = {
							add_ideas = MAN_white_movement
						}
					}
				}
				
				else = {
					SOV = { #one state soviet
						country_event = { id = RCM_Manchoukuo.17 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort

		}
		modifier = {
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}
RCM_officer_unrest_build_up = {
	RCM_unrest_against_yonai = {
		icon = revolt
		is_good = no
		activation = {
			always = no #activated by event
		}
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = JAP_consolidate_yonai_cabinet_focus
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = { character = mitsumasa_yonai ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = ROOT.yonai_unrest
	
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_subject = yes
				has_global_flag = JAP_defeated
			}
		}
	
		timeout_effect = {			
			if = {
				limit = {
					#has_stability > 0.3

		timeout_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
			activate_mission = RCM_promise_of_election_mission
			custom_effect_tooltip = next_time_halved_time_tt
			divide_variable = {
				DAYS_OF_PROMISED_ELECTION = 2
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_communist_in_government
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = n_socialism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = -0.10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = n_socialism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = n_socialism
					popularity = -0.10
				}
			}
			
			add_stability = -0.10
			add_war_support = -0.10
			add_political_power = -150
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abor
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						TAG = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						TAG = CHI
					}
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_communist_in_government
					}
				}
				has_completed_focus = CHI_declare_martial_law_focus
			}
			else = {
				hidden_trigger = {
					always = no
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 200
		}
	}
}

RCM_warlord_support_central_governmet_cat = {
	RCM_warlord_support_central_governmet = {
		icon = eng_trade_unions_support
		allowed = {
			#is_literally_china = yes
		}
		days_remove = 15
		visible = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china = yes
				}
				has_war_together_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				has_war_with = JAP
				NOT = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					any_neighbor_country = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
				}
				FROM = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					#has_idea = CHI_sov_pacthas_idea = CHI_sov_pact
					OR = {
						has_government = ROOT
						is_ai = yes
						has_completed_focus = CHI_mission_to_the_soviet_union
					}
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_german_coop
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
				}
				FROM = {
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					has_idea = CHI_german_coop
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
					OR = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						tag = USA
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
				has_war_with = JAP
				FROM = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_government = fascism
							has_idea = CHI_german_coop
						}
					}
					has_war_with = JAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					has_war_together_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			else = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		#target_array = neighbors
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_capitulated = no
				is_literally_china = yes
				has_defensive_war_with = JAP
				#has_war_together_with = ROOT
				any_enemy_country = {
					is_neighbor_of = FROM
				}
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					is_literally_china = yes
				}
				any_enemy_country = {
					is_neighbor_of = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 59999
					}
					FROM = {
						is_ai = yes
						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					}
				}
				has_equipment = { #just for show lol
					infantry_equipment > 5999
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SOV
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 29999
					}
					FROM = {
						is_ai = no
						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					}
				}
				has_equipment = { #just for show lol
					infantry_equipment > 2999
				}
			}
			else = {
				has_equipment = {
					infantry_equipment > 999
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
		#custom_effect_tooltip = "[?ROOT.send_aid_count|]"
			#add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			#	type = infantry_equipment
			#	amount = -1000
			#}
		}
		remove_trigger = { #will run remove effect and abort

		}
		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = send_aid_count_start
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = send_aid_count_start
				set_variable = {
					ROOT.send_aid_count = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					ROOT.send_aid_count = 1
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = equipment_support_cd@FROM value = 1 days = 50 }
			FROM = {
				country_event = rcm_warlord_help.1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #send more guns man!
					tag = SOV
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 59999
					}
					FROM = {

					tag = SOV

					}

		cost = 0
		#available = {
		#	hidden_trigger = {
		#		command_power > 24
		#	}
		#}
		#custom_cost_trigger = {
		#	command_power > 24
		#}
		#custom_cost_text = cp_at_least_25
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
		
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = { 
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = military_region_1_modifier scope = ROOT
				}
			}
 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}
		
		visible = { #can see
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			has_global_flag = has_military_regions_flag
			any_core_state = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = military_region_1_modifier scope = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

        days_remove = 14

		available = { #can do
			has_war_with = JAP
			check_variable = { mr_1_value > 0.04 }
		}
		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
		    if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_1_value = 0.05 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv1_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_1_value = 0.1 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv2_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_1_value = 0.15 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv3_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_1_value = 0.2 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv4_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_1_value = 0.25 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv5_tt
		    }
	    }  
		remove_trigger = { #will run remove effect and abort
		    
		}
		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
		    add_to_variable = {
			    var = mr_1_value
			    value = -0.05
			    tooltip = subtract_5_to_mr_tt
		    }
		    if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_global_flag = mr_1_max_flag
			    }
			    clr_global_flag = mr_1_max_flag
		    }
			add_political_power = @mr_cost
			add_command_power = @mr_cp_cost
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort

		}
		modifier = { #active during the course of the decision

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	invest_in_military_region_2 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = @mr_cost
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > @mr_cp_cost_trigger
			has_political_power > @mr_cost_trigger
		}
		custom_cost_text = cp_at_least_25_pp_at_least_25
		#available = {
		#	hidden_trigger = {
		#		command_power > 24
		#	}
		#}
		#custom_cost_trigger = {
		#	command_power > 24
		#}
		#custom_cost_text = cp_at_least_25
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
		
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = { 
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = military_region_2_modifier scope = ROOT
				}
			}
 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}
		
		visible = { #can see
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			has_global_flag = has_military_regions_flag
			any_core_state = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = military_region_2_modifier scope = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

        days_remove = 14

		available = { #can do
		    hidden_trigger = {
			    command_power > @mr_cp_cost_trigger
				has_political_power > @mr_cost_trigger
		    }
		    has_war_with = JAP
			check_variable = { mr_2_value < 0.26 }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = less_than_5_max_lv_mr_tt
				NOT = {
					count_triggers = {
						amount = 5
						has_global_flag = mr_1_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_2_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_3_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_4_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_5_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_6_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_7_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_8_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_9_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_10_max_flag
					}
				}	
			}	
		}

		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
		    hidden_effect = {
			    add_command_power = @mr_cp_cost_effect
				add_political_power = @mr_cost_effect
		    }
		    if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_2_value = 0.05 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv1_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_2_value = 0.1 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv2_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_2_value = 0.15 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv3_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_2_value = 0.2 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv4_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_2_value = 0.25 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv5_tt
		    }
	    } 

		remove_trigger = { #will run remove effect and abort

		}
		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
            add_to_variable = {
			    var = mr_2_value
			    value = 0.05
			    tooltip = add_5_to_mr_tt
		    }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { mr_2_value > 0.24 }
				}
				set_global_flag = mr_2_max_flag
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort

		}
		modifier = { #active during the course of the decision

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	invest_in_military_region_5 = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_trade_unions_support
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = @mr_cost
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > @mr_cp_cost_trigger
			has_political_power > @mr_cost_trigger
		}
		custom_cost_text = cp_at_least_25_pp_at_least_25
		#available = {
		#	hidden_trigger = {
		#		command_power > 24
		#	}
		#}
		#custom_cost_trigger = {
		#	command_power > 24
		#}
		#custom_cost_text = cp_at_least_25
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
		
        highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = { 
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = military_region_5_modifier scope = ROOT
				}
			}
 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		visible = { #can see
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			has_global_flag = has_military_regions_flag
			any_core_state = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = military_region_5_modifier scope = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

        days_remove = 14

		available = { #can do
		    hidden_trigger = {
			    command_power > @mr_cp_cost_trigger
				has_political_power > @mr_cost_trigger
		    }
		    has_war_with = JAP
			check_variable = { mr_5_value < 0.26 }
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = less_than_5_max_lv_mr_tt
				NOT = {
					count_triggers = {
						amount = 5
						has_global_flag = mr_1_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_2_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_3_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_4_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_5_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_6_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_7_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_8_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_9_max_flag
						has_global_flag = mr_10_max_flag
					}
				}	
			}	
		}

		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
		    hidden_effect = {
			    add_command_power = @mr_cp_cost_effect
				add_political_power = @mr_cost_effect
		    }
		    if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_5_value = 0.05 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv1_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_5_value = 0.1 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv2_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_5_value = 0.15 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv3_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_5_value = 0.2 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv4_tt
		    }
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    check_variable = { mr_5_value = 0.25 }
			    }
			    custom_effect_tooltip = this_mr_is_lv5_tt
		    }
	    } 

		remove_trigger = { #will run remove effect and abort

		}
		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
            add_to_variable = {
			    var = mr_5_value
			    value = 0.05
			    tooltip = add_5_to_mr_tt
		    }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { mr_5_value > 0.24 }
				}
				set_global_flag = mr_5_max_flag
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort

		}
		modifier = { #active during the course of the decision

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

					is_literally_china = yes
					has_war_with = jAP
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
			}
 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		visible = { #can see
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			has_global_flag = has_military_regions_flag
			any_core_state = { #1940/7 
			    is_mr6_state = yes
				is_not_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
			}
		}

        days_remove = 30

		available = { #can do
			has_war_with = JAP
		}

		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection
		    
	    } 

		remove_trigger = { #will run remove effect and abort

		}
		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
		    set_global_flag = mr_6_established_flag
		    every_core_state = {
				limit = {
					is_mr6_state = yes
					is_not_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = im_mr6_state_flag
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = military_region_6_modifier scope = ROOT
				}
				owner = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_literally_china = yes
							has_war_with = JAP
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								is_mr6_state = yes
								is_controlled_by_jap_or_its_puppet = no
							}
							add_dynamic_modifier = {
								modifier = military_region_6_modifier scope = PREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort

		}
		modifier = { #active during the course of the decision

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}

						has_war_with = jAP
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
							has_government = communism
						}

					modifier = military_region_8_modifier scope = ROOT

							}

							}

					}
				}
			}

			    var = mr_8_value
			    value = 0.15
			    tooltip = add_15_to_mr_tt
		    }
		}

		}
		modifier = { #active during the course of the decision

		}

			factor = 1
			modifier = {

				factor = 100
			}
		}

			}
		}

    chi_kham_offensive = {

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			is_literally_china = yes
		}

		available = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_250
					region = 250
				}
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_active_mission = chi_preparing_offensive }
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_250
					region = 250
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					num_owned_neighbour_states = {
						owner = ROOT
						count > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = { 
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				region = 250
			}

 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = @offsive_days

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					is_literally_china = yes
					OR = {
						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				}
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			}
			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_250
					region = 250
				}
			}
			NOT = {
                has_active_mission = chi_kham_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			activate_mission = chi_preparing_offensive
			set_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
				}
				activate_mission = chi_kham_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 150
					}
					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
			#		171 = { is_controlled_by = SPD }
			#	}
			#	add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }
			#}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						region = 250
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.big_china
							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
							region = 250
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}  
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			}
			#modifier = {
			#	factor = 10
			#	divisions_in_state = {
			#		state = 171
			#		size > 0
			#	}
			#	NOT = {

			#	}
			#}
		}

				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 247
					}
					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
			#		171 = { is_controlled_by = SPD }
			#	}
			#	add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }
			#}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						region = 247
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.big_china
							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
							region = 247
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}  
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.big_china
					has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					region = 247
					controller = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					num_owned_neighbour_states = {
						owner = ROOT
						count > 2
					}
				}
			}
			#modifier = {
			#	factor = 10
			#	divisions_in_state = {
			#		state = 171
			#		size > 0
			#	}
			#	NOT = {
			#		has_full_control_of_state = 171
			#	}
			#}
		}

    chi_southeast_offensive = {

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			is_literally_china = yes
		}

		available = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_164
					region = 164
				}
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_active_mission = chi_preparing_offensive }
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_164
					region = 164
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					num_owned_neighbour_states = {
						owner = ROOT
						count > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = { 
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				region = 164
			}

 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = @offsive_days

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					is_literally_china = yes
					OR = {
						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				}
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			}
			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_164
					region = 164
				}
			}
			NOT = {
                has_active_mission = chi_southeast_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			activate_mission = chi_preparing_offensive
			set_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
				}
				activate_mission = chi_southeast_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 164
					}
					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
			#if = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
			#		171 = { is_controlled_by = SPD }
			#	}
			#	add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }
			#}
		}

			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag

	chi_preparing_offensive = {

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			is_literally_china = yes
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = @offsive_days

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			hidden_trigger = {
                OR = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					AND = {
						is_ai = no
						is_literally_china = yes
						OR = {
							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			}
			has_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
		}
	}

							modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
						}

							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
							has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_250
					region = 250
				}
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			effect_tooltip = {
                for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.big_china
					if = {
						limit = {
							region = 250
						}
						clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						remove_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	CHI_inch_blood_up_decision = { #perk increase
		targets = {
			PRC CHI SIK PLM GXC YUN SHX XSM XIK SIC GUD HPC NEA SHD NXM SHC GSM EGM TNG KHR HMI XIA KRS ATM SUY D01 D02 D03 D04 D05 D06 D07 D08 D09 D10 D11 D12 D13 D14 D15
		}
		target_trigger = {
			#Target is FROM
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_1
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_2
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_3
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_4
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_5
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_6
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_7
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_8
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_9
					has_idea = CHI_inch_blood_10
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					exists = yes
					has_country_flag = CHI_inch_blood_up_decision_flag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						JAP = {
							is_ai = yes
						}
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					CHI_inch_blood_up_trigger_for_double_AI = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_ai = yes
						JAP = {
							is_ai = no
							OR = {
								has_completed_focus = JAP_placate_military_focus
								has_completed_focus = JAP_Sonno_Tokkan_focus
							}
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					CHI_inch_blood_up_trigger_for_AI_china = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					CHI_inch_blood_up_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			is_ai = yes
			capital_scope = {
				is_on_continent = south_america
			}
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					exists = yes
					has_country_flag = CHI_inch_blood_up_decision_flag
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 9000
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CHI_inch_blood_up_decision_flag
			FROM = {
				CHI_inch_blood_level_up = yes
			}
		}
	}

socialism_on_the_rise = {
	prepare_for_socialist_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		available = {
			n_socialism > 0.1
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = preparation_for_n_socialism_civil_war }
			has_idea_with_trait = socialist_idealist
			check_has_focus_tree_to_switch_to_n_socialism = yes
			NOT = { has_government = n_socialism }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 50

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	expand_civil_socialist_support = {

		icon = generic_civil_support

		visible = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war
				has_country_flag = open_up_political_discourse_n_socialism
			}
			has_idea_with_trait = socialist_idealist
			check_has_focus_tree_to_switch_to_n_socialism = yes
			NOT = { has_government = n_socialism }
		}

		fire_only_once = no

		cost = 25

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			n_socialism_drift = 0.02 #0.02
			stability_weekly = -0.03
			political_power_gain = -0.2
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	army_support_for_socialist_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = socialist_idealist
			check_has_focus_tree_to_switch_to_n_socialism = yes
			NOT = { has_government = n_socialism }
		}

		fire_only_once = no

		cost = 50

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			command_power_gain = -0.02
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = less_than }
				}
				set_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { var = army_support_var value = 0.1 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				}

	ignite_the_socialist_civil_war = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_stability < 0.5
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war
			has_idea_with_trait = socialist_idealist
			check_has_focus_tree_to_switch_to_n_socialism = yes
			NOT = { has_government = n_socialism }
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 50

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@fascism
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@democratic
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@neutrality
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = party_popularity@communism
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = civil_war_size_var
				value = army_support_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = civil_war_size_var
						value = 0.3
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = civil_war_size_var
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = n_socialism
				ideology = ROOT
				size = civil_war_size_var
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					has_trait = hidden_sympathies
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = preparation_for_socialist_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = military_support_for_socialist_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = civil_support_for_socialist_civil_war
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

			    }
			}
			random_list = {
				var:gud_army_deflect_chance = {
					if = { 
						limit = {
							tag = GUD 
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = GUD_get_annexed_or_puppeted_tt
					}
					country_event = { id = gud.6 }

					}
				}
				var:gud_army_keep_chance = {
					set_global_flag = buy_gud_army_fail
					CHI = { country_event = gud.14 }
				}  
			}
			
			if = {
			    limit = { 
					check_variable = { gud_army_deflect_chance < 1 }
				}  
			    set_global_flag = buy_gud_army_fail
                CHI = { country_event = gud.14 }
			}		
		}
	}

economy_decisions = {
	monetary_reform_decision = {
		icon = generic_economy
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 120 # Stays for 5 days before being removed
		days_re_enable = 0 # Will show up in the interface and can be selected again after 5 days
		cost = 25
		highlight_states = { #These states will be highlighted

		}
		visible = { #can see
			OR = {
				has_idea = unstable_economy
				has_idea = warlord_economy
			}
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = CHI_monetary_reform
				has_completed_focus = WRL_monetary_reform
			}
		}
		available = { #can do
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = unstable_economy
				}
				has_idea = unstable_economy
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = warlord_economy
				}
				has_idea = warlord_economy
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { #run effect on selection

		}
		remove_trigger = { #will run remove effect and abort

		}
		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = unstable_economy
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = unstable_economy
					add_idea = civilian_economy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = warlord_economy
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = warlord_economy
					add_idea = civilian_economy
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = has_taken_monetary_reform_decision
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort

		}
		modifier = { #active during the course of the decision
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.15
			political_power_gain = -0.1
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 2000
		}
	}
}

		remove_effect = { #run effect when removed/finished
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = prepared_for_operation
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = prepared_for_operation_tt
		}
		cancel_trigger = { #will abort

		}
		modifier = { #active during the course of the decision
			command_power_gain = -0.15
			
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 500#guo
		}
	}
	RCM_communist_amass_support_mission = {#GUO
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = RCM_communist_amass_support_mission_time_zz #GUO # Stays for 5 days before being removed
		#days_re_enable = 25 # Will show up in the interface and can be selected again after 5 days
		is_good = yes
		allowed = {
			is_literally_china = yes
		}
		available = { #can doc
			event_target:amass_support_flag_temp = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = commie_ridden_states
					}
					NOT = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		activation = {
			always = no #activate through scripted gui
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
					country_event = RCM_communist_uprising.5
				}
				JAP = {
					country_event = RCM_communist_uprising.5
				}
				
				event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
					country_event = RCM_communist_uprising.5
				}
			}
			#random_state = {
			#	limit = {
			#		has_state_flag = amass_support_flag_temp
			#	}
			#} #guo
			event_target:amass_support_flag_temp = {
				owner = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									tag = JAP
									tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
									tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
								}
							}
						}
						country_event = RCM_communist_uprising.5
					}
				}
				THIS = {
					add_core_of = ROOT
					
					if = {
					limit = { has_state_flag = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_state_flag }
						add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_1 scope = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
						#add_state_modifier = {
						#	modifier = {
						#		local_supplies = 0.15
						#	}
						#}
					}
					
				}
				clr_state_flag = amass_support_flag_temp
				set_state_flag = commie_amassed_support
			}
			add_war_support = 0.005
			event_target:amass_support_flag_temp = {
				clear_global_event_target = amass_support_flag_temp
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:amass_support_flag_temp = {
						WTT_is_potential_political_struggle_state = yes
					}
					has_country_flag = wtt_political_struggle
				}
				#Add random state support for ROOT
				WTT_random_support_chance_increase_for_ROOT_in_state = yes

				hidden_effect = {
					#Save relevant event targets. Need to be done before updating state support
					save_event_target_as = state
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							PREV = { has_state_flag = majority_political_platform_@PREV }
						}
						save_event_target_as = majority_country
					}

					#Update state support
					WTT_recalculate_state_support_for_ROOT = yes

					#Status events
					WTT_fire_add_support_status_events = yes

					#Recalc all support
					WTT_political_struggle_recalculate_support = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
	}
	RCM_amass_local_communist_support = {#guo
		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns
		
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {

				hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = original_tib_state } }
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_1 scope = event_target:WTT_communist_china }

		visible = {

			any_owned_state = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				or = { is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } is_core_of = CHI is_core_of = PRC has_state_flag = original_chi_state }
				hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_state_flag = original_tib_state } }
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_1 scope = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
					hidden_trigger = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_2 scope = event_target:WTT_communist_china } }
				}
			}
		}
		available = {

				or = { is_in_array = { global.small_china = This.id } is_core_of = CHI is_core_of = PRC has_state_flag = original_chi_state }

				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_1 scope = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
					hidden_trigger = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_2 scope = event_target:WTT_communist_china } }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_active_mission = RCM_communist_amass_support_mission
			}
		}
		cost = RCM_communist_amass_support_mission_cost_zz#guo
		#days_remove = 7
		#days_re_enable = 7
		#fire_only_once = yes
		modifier = {

		}
		remove_effect = {

		}
		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				
				save_global_event_target_as = amass_support_flag_temp
				
				set_state_flag = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_state_flag#guo
				effect_tooltip = {#guo
					custom_effect_tooltip = after_done_amass_support_flag_temp
					add_core_of = root
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = snl_PRC_dyn_land_reform_1 scope = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
					add_state_modifier = {
						modifier = {
							local_supplies = 0.15
						}
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = RCM_communist_amass_support_mission
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 350#GUO
		}

						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = JAP_ai_behavior
							option = OKADA_STAYS_TOHOKAI
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				has_political_power < 60
				command_power < 75
			}
			else = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		days_remove = 30

		visible = {

			OR = {
				has_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_1
				has_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_2
			}
			NOT = { has_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_3 }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_placate_military_focus }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = JAP_strengthen_civilian_government }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_1
					add_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_2
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = pm_ass_lowered_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_2
					add_idea = JAP_bribe_the_tokko_3
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = pm_ass_free_tt
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.25
		}
		complete_effect = {

		}
	}
}

					NOT = {
						has_variable = global.I_am_prolly_commie_china
					}
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 1007
						owns_state = 1006
					}
					set_variable = {
						global.I_am_prolly_commie_china = THIS
					}
				}
			}		
			random_other_country = { #I started this
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = ROOT
					}

						is_subject_of = PREV
					}

						NOT = {
							tag = SOV
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = NK_LORD_I_exist_haha_but_YOU_STARTED_IT
					}
					NOT = {
						country_exists = global.south_KOR_overlord
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = SK_LORD_I_exist_haha_but_YOU_STARTED_IT
				set_variable = {
					global.south_KOR_overlord = THIS
				}			
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = SK_LORD_I_exist_haha_but_YOU_STARTED_IT
					country_exists = global.south_KOR_overlord
				}
				var:global.south_KOR_overlord = {					
					country_event = RCM_KOR_country_formation.11 #alert this guy (prolly US) that we (prolly SOV) are doing sketchy things in KOR	
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = SK_LORD_I_exist_haha_but_YOU_STARTED_IT } #simply to check who started it, not whether or not it exist
					country_exists = global.south_KOR_overlord
				}
				var:global.south_KOR_overlord = {					
					country_event = RCM_KOR_country_formation.6 #notify prolly US
				}
			}

				}
			}

			}

				is_in_faction_with = KOR
			}

		}

		}
